(Notice under Section 72 of the Indian Partnership Act, 1932)
Retirement of a Partner from the Firm M/s. Marcus Pharmaceuticals
Name and place of business of the Firm
:
		
		
		

M/s. Marcus Pharmaceuticals, 					
No. 67A, 5th Street, 						
Kavignar Kannadasan Nagar, 					
Chennai-600 089.

From the date of inception of the Firm, till 17th February 2019, the Partners of M/s. Marcus Pharmaceuticals
were Mrs. S. Yuvarani and Mr. T. Pravin Kumar, on 18-2-2019, a new Partner, namely Mrs. P. Sangeetha, W/o T. Pravin Kumar,
residing at No. 37-J, Manthoppu Colony, Ashok Nagar, Chennai-600 083, joined the Firm and thereby the Partnership Firm was
reconstituted. Subsequently, on 19th February 2019, Mrs. S. Yuvarani, retired from the Firm by executing a Deed of Retirement
dated 19th February 2019.
Name and place of residence
:
of the Retiring Partner 		
		
		
Date of retirement

S. Yuvarani, W/o. V. Chennakesavalu, 			
A1, Pandian Apartments,

T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017.

:
of the Continuing Partners 		
		
		

1. T. Pravin Kumar, S/o Thangavel Udayar,				
2. P. Sangeetha, W/o. T. Pravin Kumar, 				
Both residing at No. 37-J, Manthoppu Colony, 			
Ashok Nagar, Chennai-600 083.

The above ‘Continuing Partners’, shall continue to operate the business under the name and style of M/s. Marcus Pharmaceuticals’
as consented by the Retiring Partner. Be it known that the rights and liabilities of the continuing Firm and that of My client, the
retiring partner Mrs. S. Yuvarani are mutually exclusive of each other from the date of the retirement above mentioned. If any
person has any liability or objection or any other issue that they deem important wishes to bring it to the notice of the Retiring
Partner, he/she may directly contact the undersigned in person or otherwise within 15 days from the date of this notice. No claim
or issue or objection shall be entertained after such date. This notice is issued in the interests of the interested parties to the firm
and general public.
High Court Buildings, Chennai-600 104.
